<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:meager.html>meager</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">meagerer</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">meagerest</b>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_and_British_English_spelling_differences" class="extiw" title="w:American and British English spelling differences">American spelling</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>Having little flesh; lean; thin.</li>
<li>Poor, deficient or inferior in amount, quality or extent
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">paltry</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">scanty</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">inadequate</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">measly</span></span></dd>
<dd><i>A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meager.html>meager</a></b> piece of cake in one bite.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1607</b>,  Thomas Walkington,  <cite>The Optick Glasse of Humors, or, The touchstone of a golden <a href = vnd.unilang:temperaturen.html>temperature</a>, or ...</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=MnTsAAAAMAAJamp;pg=PT139amp;q=meager">[1]</a></sup>, page 54:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">...that begets many ugly and deformed phantasies in the braine, which being also hot and <a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>drie</a> in the second extenuates and <a href = vnd.unilang:makes.html>makes</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meager.html>meager</a></b> the body extraordinarily, ...</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1637</b>,  William Shakespeare,  <cite>The most excellent <a href = vnd.unilang:historie.html>Historie</a> of the Merchant of Venice: With the extreame crueltie of <i>Shylocke</i>...</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=0iDPAAAAMAAJamp;q=meager">[2]</a></sup>, page E5:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Nor none of <a href = vnd.unilang:thee.html>thee</a> thou pale and common drudge tween <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a>: but thou, thou <b><a href = vnd.unilang:meager.html>meager</a></b> lead which rather threatnest then dost promise ought...</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">set theory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Of a set: such that, considered as a subset of a (usually larger) topological space, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in a precise sense small or negligible.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mineralogy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Dry and harsh to the touch (e.g., as chalk).</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mechaniek.html>mechaniek</a> (56722)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">mecanique</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:mechanicus.html>mechanicus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">of or belonging to <a href = vnd.unilang:machines.html>machines</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:mechanics.html>mechanics</a>, inventive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Î¼Î·ÏÎ±Î½Î¹ÎºÏÏ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mÄkhanikÃ³s</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">pertaining to <a href = vnd.unilang:machines.html>machines</a> or contrivance, mechanic, ingenious, inventive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Î¼Î·ÏÎ±Î½Î®</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mÄkhaná¸</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">a machine, contrivance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">machine</i>.

<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">Dutch Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:mechanisch" class="extiw" title="w:nl:mechanisch"><a href = vnd.unilang:mechanisch.html>mechanisch</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:mechanisch" class="extiw" title="w:nl:mechanisch">Wikipedia <sup>nl</sup></a></span></div>

***mede.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mede.html>mede</a> (9496)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">mithi</i>, stressed variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">mit</i> (from which <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a></i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*midi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mede.html>mede</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>co-
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:mede.html>Mede</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gemaakt.html>gemaakt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> (...).</i>  |  Co-made by (sponsered by).</dd></dl></li>
<li>With someone or something else (<a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a>)</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*medu</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*medo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*meduz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>mead <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">fermented <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> made from honey</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

***mee.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a> (100)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mede.html>mede</a></i> with the frequent loss of intervocalic <i>-d-</i> (cf. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kou.html>kou</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:vs.html>vs</a>. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koude.html>koude</a></i> ["cold"]; <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slee.html>slee</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:vs.html>vs</a>. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slede.html>slede</a></i> ["sleigh"]). The forms <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mee.html>mee</a></i> and <i><a href = vnd.unilang:mede.html>mede</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> subsequently distributed to different senses.
</p>

***meerkat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:meerkat.html>meerkat</a> (103143)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">meercatte</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss">monkey, ape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">â</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*merikatta</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kat.html>kat</a></i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">merikazza</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Meerkatze</i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meerkat.html>meerkat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meerkatten.html>meerkatten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:meerkat.html>meerkatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A guenon, vervet, talapoin or patas; one of a number of <a href = vnd.unilang:monkeys.html>monkeys</a> of the genus <i>Cercopithecus</i>, or of the tribe <i>Cercopithecini</i>.
